2011-03-31 18:15:37 +0200 (Thu, 31 Mar 2011), revision 3441, ekolin
Add support for additional locally defined replacement filters to the xargs-task.
U   knopflerfish.org/trunk/ant/xargs.xml

2011-03-31 07:52:02 +0200 (Thu, 31 Mar 2011), revision 3440, ekolin
The ant helper build file, xargs.xml, has been revised; the old targets has been repalced with a single task named 'xargs'. The new xargs-target supports a nested bundles-element that may contain file-sets selecting the set of bundles to use to determine the actual file name of the highest version of a bundle. By default the new xargs-target uses the path in the gosgJars attribute for this, which works nicely when the URLs in gosgJars are file URLs but for other kind of URLs the nested bundles element must be used to specify the set of bundles available on the non-file URLs.
U   knopflerfish.org/trunk/ant/src/org/knopflerfish/ant/taskdefs/bundle/BundleLocator.java
U   knopflerfish.org/trunk/ant/xargs.xml
U   knopflerfish.org/trunk/build.xml
U   knopflerfish.org/trunk/osgi/build.xml

2011-03-27 18:13:35 +0200 (Sun, 27 Mar 2011), revision 3439, ekolin
The bundleLocator task now takes a bundlePath attribute with a value that is a semicolon separated path of URLs to bundle repositories. If present the task adds a file set to itself for each URL of type 'file:' in the given bundlePath (the file set will selec all jar-files (bundles) and be rooted at the path of the file-URL).
